
makeblastdb -in temp/database/database_exons_1.fa -input_type fasta -dbtype nucl -parse_seqids -blastdb_version 5 -max_file_sz 4GB -out temp/database/database
blastn -db temp/database/database -query temp/targetome/targetome_norm_query.fa -task blastn-short -word_size 11 -strand plus -evalue 1000000000 -max_target_seqs 1000000000 -out temp/BLAST/BLAST_norm_exons_1.txt 2>/dev/null
grep -e "Query=" -e ">" -e "Sbjct" temp/BLAST/BLAST_norm_exons_1.txt >> temp/BLAST/BLAST_norm_exons.txt
rm temp/BLAST/BLAST_norm_exons_1.txt
